***obelisk.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:obelisk.html>obelisk</a> (37963)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>1569. From <span class="etylcleanup"><span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_French" class="extiw" title="w:Middle French">Middle French</a></span></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="frm">obelisque</i>, from <span class="etylcleanup"><span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">obeliscus</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:obelisk.html>obelisk</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etylcleanup"><span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ancient_Greek" class="extiw" title="w:Ancient Greek">Ancient Greek</a></span></span> <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">ὀβελίσκος</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">obelískos</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, diminutive of <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">ὀβελός</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">obelós</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">needle</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:obelisk.html>obelisk</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">obelisks</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>A tall, square, tapered, stone monolith topped with a pyramidal point, frequently used as a monument.
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>2012</b> January 1,  <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Henry_Petroski" class="extiw" title="w:Henry Petroski"><a href = vnd.unilang:henry.html>Henry</a> Petroski</a>,  “The Washington Monument”, in  <cite><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/American_Scientist" class="extiw" title="w:American Scientist">American Scientist</a></cite> | <sup><a rel="nofollow" class="external autonumber" href="http://www.americanscientist.org/issues/pub/the-washington-monument">[1]</a></sup>, volume 100, number 1, page 16:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">The Washington Monument <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> often described as an <b><a href = vnd.unilang:obelisk.html>obelisk</a></b>, and sometimes <a href = vnd.unilang:even.html>even</a> as a  | true <b><a href = vnd.unilang:obelisk.html>obelisk</a></b>, |  <a href = vnd.unilang:even.html>even</a> though it <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> not. A true <b><a href = vnd.unilang:obelisk.html>obelisk</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> a monolith, a <a href = vnd.unilang:pylon.html>pylon</a> formed out of a single piece of stone.</span></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">printing</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> The dagger sign (†), especially when used as a reference mark.</li></ol>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Zelfstandig_naamwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:zelfstandig.html>Zelfstandig</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:naamwoord.html>naamwoord</a></i></span></h4>
<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:obelisk.html>obelisk</a></b> <span style="background-color: f8f9fa;border-radius: 2px;border: 1px solid c8ccd1;padding: 0 0.2em 0 0.1em;font-style: italic">m</span>
</p>
<ol><li><a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:stenen.html>stenen</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:vaak.html>vaak</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:granieten.html>granieten</a>, gedenknaald <a href = vnd.unilang:zoals.html>zoals</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:deze.html>deze</a> eertijds in <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:oude.html>Oude</a> Egypte <a href = vnd.unilang:opgericht.html>opgericht</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:werden.html>werden</a>
<dl><dd><ul><li><i><a href = vnd.unilang:er.html>Er</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:zijn.html>zijn</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:obelisken.html>obelisken</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:verplaatst.html>verplaatst</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:naar.html>naar</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:rome.html>Rome</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:en.html>en</a> Constantinopel.</i> </li></ul></dd></dl></li></ol>

***ober.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:ober.html>ober</a> (4721)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de"><a href = vnd.unilang:ober.html>Ober</a></i>, short for <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Oberkellner</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">head waiter</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Compare Dutch <i class="Latn mention" lang="de"><a href = vnd.unilang:kelner.html>kelner</a></i>, which <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> also borrowed from German. In both Dutch and German, the distinction between <i><a href = vnd.unilang:ober.html>ober</a>/<a href = vnd.unilang:ober.html>Ober</a></i> and <i><a href = vnd.unilang:kelner.html>kelner</a>/Kellner</i> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> now neglected.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ober.html>ober</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:obers.html>obers</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ober.html>obertje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>waiter
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:laten.html>Laten</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:we.html>we</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:ober.html>ober</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:roepen.html>roepen</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:dan.html>dan</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:kunnen.html>kunnen</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:we.html>we</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:bestellen.html>bestellen</a>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">Let's call the <b>waiter</b>, then <a href = vnd.unilang:we.html>we</a> can order.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Zelfstandig_naamwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:zelfstandig.html>Zelfstandig</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:naamwoord.html>naamwoord</a></i></span></h4>
<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:ober.html>ober</a></b> <span style="background-color: f8f9fa;border-radius: 2px;border: 1px solid c8ccd1;padding: 0 0.2em 0 0.1em;font-style: italic">m</span>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_French" class="extiw" title="w:Old French">Old French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro">obscur</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">obscūrus</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">dark, dusky, indistinct</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Akin to English <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">obscure</i> and German <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">obskur</i>.

***obsessie.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:obsessie.html>obsessie</a> (5084)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">obsessiō</i>, formed synchronically in Dutch as <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:obsederen.html>obsederen</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:-ie.html>-ie</a></i>.

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_High_German" class="extiw" title="w:Old High German">Old High German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="goh">ahto</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*ahtōu</i>. Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de"><a href = vnd.unilang:acht.html>acht</a></i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Dutch_language" class="extiw" title="w:Dutch language">Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:acht.html>acht</a></i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">eight</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Swedish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Swedish language">Swedish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="sv">åtta</i>.
</p>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">ochtent</i>, earlier <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">ochte</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*ūhto</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*unhtwǭ</i>. ***oddball.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:oddball.html>oddball</a> (39137)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Compound of <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">odd</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">ball</i>. Attested since the 1940s, with the adjective appearing earlier than the noun.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:oddball.html>oddball</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">oddballs</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>An eccentric or unusual person.
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1964</b>,  <a href = vnd.unilang:earl.html>Earl</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:warren.html>Warren</a> et alia,  <cite>Report of the President's Commission on the Assassination of President John F. Kennedy</cite> | <sup><a rel="nofollow" class="external autonumber" href="http://www.worldcat.org/title/report-of-the-presidents-commission-on-the-assassination-of-president-john-f-kennedy/">[1]</a></sup>, page 685:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">Miss Quinn thought that Oswald <a href = vnd.unilang:spoken.html>spoke</a> Russian well in view of his lack of formal training; she found the evening uninteresting. Donovan, with whom she <a href = vnd.unilang:had.html>had</a> a date <a href = vnd.unilang:later.html>later</a>, testified that she <a href = vnd.unilang:told.html>told</a> him that Oswald <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> “kind of an <b><a href = vnd.unilang:oddball.html>oddball</a></b>.”</span></div></dd></dl></div></li>
<li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1989</b>,  <a href = vnd.unilang:maris.html>Maris</a> Soule,  <cite>Storybook Hero</cite>, page 5:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">"She's different, <a href = vnd.unilang:mister.html>mister</a>. A real <b><a href = vnd.unilang:oddball.html>oddball</a></b>, if you know what I mean. But your little girl would love her. All kids love the Doll Lady."</span></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">neuroscience</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A deviant stimulus that appears among repetitive <a href = vnd.unilang:stimuli.html>stimuli</a> during an experiment, to trigger an event-related potential in the participant.</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">eccentric or unusual person</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span><span class="ib-colon sense-qualifier-colon">:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:kook.html>kook</a></span>, <span class="Latn" lang="en">odd duck</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="en">odd duck</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="en">strange fish</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="en">queer fish</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:weirdo.html>weirdo</a></span>; see also Thesaurus:strange person</li></ul>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:oddball.html>oddball</a></strong> (<i>not comparable</i>)
</p>
<ol><li>Exotic, not mainstream.
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1984</b>,  <a href = vnd.unilang:steven.html>Steven</a> K. Roberts,  <cite>The Complete Guide to Microsystem Management</cite>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">An <b><a href = vnd.unilang:oddball.html>oddball</a></b> word processor, for example, might never be supported by such helpful tools as spelling <a href = vnd.unilang:checkers.html>checkers</a>, indexing programs, footnote utilities,...</span></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li></ol>
</body> 
***odds.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:odds.html>odds</a> (114832)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">odd</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">uneven, strange</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:odds.html>odds</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="plural number">pl</abbr></span> (<i>plural only</i>)
</p>
<ol><li>The ratio of the probability of an event happening to that of it not happening.
<dl><dd><i>I'd say the <b><a href = vnd.unilang:odds.html>odds</a></b> are strongly in favor of the sun <a href = vnd.unilang:rising.html>rising</a> tomorrow morning.</i></dd></dl></li>
<li>The ratio of winnings to stake in betting situations.</li></ol>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:odds.html>odds</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">plural of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Latn mention" lang="en">odd</i></span></span></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li>The word "<a href = vnd.unilang:odds.html>odds</a>" <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> formerly sometimes used with a singular verb, e.g. (Stephen S. Foster) "If there be any difference in the two crimes, the <a href = vnd.unilang:odds.html>odds</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> in favor of the foreign enslaver."</li></ul>
</body>

***odious.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:odious.html>odious</a> (27521)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Anglo-Norman_language" class="extiw" title="w:Anglo-Norman language">Anglo-Norman</a></span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_French" class="extiw" title="w:Old French">Old French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro">odieus</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">odiōsus</i>, from <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">odium</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">hate</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:odious.html>odious</a></strong> (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en comparative-form-of" lang="en">more <a href = vnd.unilang:odious.html>odious</a></b>, <i>superlative</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en superlative-form-of" lang="en">most <a href = vnd.unilang:odious.html>odious</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>Arousing or meriting strong dislike, aversion, or intense displeasure.
<dl><dd><i>Scrubbing the <a href = vnd.unilang:toilet.html>toilet</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> an <b><a href = vnd.unilang:odious.html>odious</a></b> task.</i></dd></dl>
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1903</b>,  <a href = vnd.unilang:sir.html>Sir</a> Arthur Conan Doyle,  “The Adventure of the Solitary Cyclist”, in  <cite>The Return of Sherlock Holmes</cite> | <sup><a href="https://en.wikisource.org/wiki/The_Adventure_of_the_Solitary_Cyclist" class="extiw" title="s:The Adventure of the Solitary Cyclist">Wikisource</a></sup>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">"He <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> a dreadful person, a bully to everyone else, but to <a href = vnd.unilang:me.html>me</a> something infinitely worse. He made <b><a href = vnd.unilang:odious.html>odious</a></b> love to <a href = vnd.unilang:me.html>me</a>, boasted of his wealth, <a href = vnd.unilang:said.html>said</a> that if I married him I would have the finest <a href = vnd.unilang:diamonds.html>diamonds</a> in London, and finally, when I would have nothing to do with him, he seized <a href = vnd.unilang:me.html>me</a> in his arms one day after dinner <a href = vnd.unilang:--.html>--</a> he <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> hideously strong <a href = vnd.unilang:--.html>--</a> and he swore that he would not let <a href = vnd.unilang:me.html>me</a> go until I <a href = vnd.unilang:had.html>had</a> kissed him."</span></div></dd></dl></div></li>
<li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1818</b>,  <a href = vnd.unilang:mary.html>Mary</a> Shelley,  chapter 6, in  <cite><a href = vnd.unilang:frankenstein.html>Frankenstein</a></cite> | <sup><a rel="nofollow" class="external autonumber" href="http://ebooks.adelaide.edu.au/s/shelley/mary/s53f/chapter6.html">[1]</a></sup>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">He <a href = vnd.unilang:looks.html>looks</a> upon study as an <b><a href = vnd.unilang:odious.html>odious</a></b> fetter; his time <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> spent in the open air, climbing the hills or rowing on the lake.</span></div></dd></dl></div></li>
<li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1750</b>,  Thomas Morell (<a href = vnd.unilang:lyrics.html>lyrics</a>), George Frideric <a href = vnd.unilang:handel.html>Handel</a> (music),  “'Theodora'” | <sup><a rel="nofollow" class="external autonumber" href="http://opera.stanford.edu/iu/libretti/theodora.htm">[2]</a></sup>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">I own no crime, unless it be a crime to've hindered you from perpetrating that which would have made you <b><a href = vnd.unilang:odious.html>odious</a></b> to mankind, at least the fairest <a href = vnd.unilang:half.html>half</a>.</span></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li>Nouns to which "<a href = vnd.unilang:odious.html>odious</a>" <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> often applied: debt, <a href = vnd.unilang:man.html>man</a>, character, crime, task, comparison, woman, person, vice, word, act.</li></ul>

<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="en">detestable</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="en">hated</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="en">reviled</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="en">unsavory</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="en">contemptible</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="en">despicable</span></li></ul>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

***oer.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:oer.html>oer</a> (90087)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Low_German" class="extiw" title="w:Low German">Low German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nds"><a href = vnd.unilang:uur.html>Uur</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*ōra</i>, <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*ūra-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">ferriferous sand</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, possibly from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*(s)wūr-</i>.  However, compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Irish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Irish language">Irish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="ga">úir</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">soil, earth</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> and <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*auraz</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:wet.html>wet</a> earth, sand, mud</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.

<p>Compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_High_German" class="extiw" title="w:Old High German">Old High German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="goh">uralt</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_English" class="extiw" title="w:Old English">Old English</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ang">oreald</i>. Equivalent to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:oer-.html>oer-</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:oud.html>oud</a></i>. <span id="attentionseekingnl" class="attentionseeking" lang="nl" title="Is this modelled after German or inherited from PWgmc?"></span>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:oever.html>oever</a> (10028)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:oever.html>oever</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*uovar</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*ōferaz</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:oever.html>oever</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:oevers.html>oevers</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:oever.html>oevertje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>bank (as in riverbank), shore (e.g. of a lake)

***oeverloos.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:oeverloos.html>oeverloos</a> (102276)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:oever.html>oever</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">riverbank</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-loos</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">-less, without</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:oeverloos.html>oeverloos</a></strong> (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:oeverloos.html>oeverlozer</a></b>, <i>superlative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:meest.html>meest</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:oeverloos.html>oeverloos</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl">oeverloost</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>shoreless</li>
<li>continuing on and on without any progress or result; boundless
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ik.html>Ik</a> word <a href = vnd.unilang:moe.html>moe</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:alle.html>alle</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:oeverloos.html>oeverloze</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:discussies.html>discussies</a> in <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:politiek.html>politiek</a>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">I'm getting tired of all the discussions <b>without result</b> in politics.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***ofer.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:ofer.html>ofer</a> (102274)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*uber</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*upér</i>, a comparative form of <i>*upo</i>.
</p><p><i>Germanic cognates:</i> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Saxon" class="extiw" title="w:Old Saxon">Old Saxon</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="osx">oƀar</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Dutch_language" class="extiw" title="w:Dutch language">Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:over.html>over</a></i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_High_German" class="extiw" title="w:Old High German">Old High German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="goh">ubar</i> (whence <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">über</i>), <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Norse" class="extiw" title="w:Old Norse">Old <a href = vnd.unilang:norse.html>Norse</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="non">yfir</i> (whence <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Swedish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Swedish language">Swedish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="sv">över</i>), <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Gothic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Gothic language">Gothic</a></span> <i class="Goth mention" lang="got">𐌿𐍆𐌰𐍂</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="got-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ufar</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p><p><i>Indo-European cognates:</i> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ancient_Greek" class="extiw" title="w:Ancient Greek">Ancient Greek</a></span> <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">ὑπέρ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">hupér</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la"><a href = vnd.unilang:super.html>super</a></i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Irish" class="extiw" title="w:Old Irish">Old Irish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="sga">for</i> (<span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Welsh_language" class="extiw" title="w:Welsh language">Welsh</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="cy">gor-</i>).
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Adverb">Adverb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latinx headword" lang="ang"><a href = vnd.unilang:ofer.html>ofer</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><a href = vnd.unilang:over.html>over</a>, above</li></ol>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Preposition">Preposition</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latinx headword" lang="ang"><a href = vnd.unilang:ofer.html>ofer</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">+dative, of a location</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> <a href = vnd.unilang:over.html>over</a>, above, beyond</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">+accusative, of motion</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> <a href = vnd.unilang:over.html>over</a>, across</li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*ōferaz</i>.
</p>

</p>
